\fi

\KeywordTok{options}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{max.print =} \DecValTok{99999}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{#import MongoDB collection into R}
\NormalTok{db <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{mongo}\NormalTok{(}
  \DataTypeTok{collection =} \StringTok{"final1"}\NormalTok{,}
  \DataTypeTok{db =} \StringTok{"analysis"}\NormalTok{,}
  \DataTypeTok{url =} \StringTok{"mongodb://localhost:27017/"}\NormalTok{,}
  \DataTypeTok{verbose =} \OtherTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{,}
  \DataTypeTok{options =} \KeywordTok{ssl_options}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{#count observations}
\NormalTok{db}\OperatorTok{$}\KeywordTok{count}\NormalTok{()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 1813
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# put environment into proper dataset - makes it easy to get an overview of nested table}
\NormalTok{df <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{db}\OperatorTok{$}\KeywordTok{find}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{'\{\}'}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{#take a quick look into the dataset}
\CommentTok{#glimpse(df)}

\CommentTok{# Flatten table}
\NormalTok{datacomplete <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{df }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{flatten}\NormalTok{()}


\CommentTok{#Remove noise}
\NormalTok{datacomplete1<-datacomplete[}\OperatorTok{!}\NormalTok{(datacomplete}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{finalannotationcontentcategory}\OperatorTok{==}\StringTok{"Noise"}\NormalTok{),]}


\CommentTok{# select only important columns from full dataset and save into a new data frame}
\CommentTok{# my_data <- as_tibble(datacomplete)}
\NormalTok{final_data <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{datacomplete1 }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{select}\NormalTok{(app_name, country_code, country, }\DataTypeTok{content_category =}\NormalTok{ finalannotationcontentcategory, }\DataTypeTok{sentiment =}\NormalTok{ finalannotationsentiment, }\DataTypeTok{gender =}\NormalTok{ finalannotationgender, created_at, }\DataTypeTok{text =}\NormalTok{ full_text)}

\NormalTok{final_data}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{obtain-month-year-from-the-original-date}{%
\subsubsection{Obtain month-year from the original
date}\label{obtain-month-year-from-the-original-date}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{tweets_date <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.POSIXct}\NormalTok{(final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{created_at, }\DataTypeTok{format =} \StringTok{"%a %b %e %T %z %Y"}\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{## Index each tweet by the day of its creation}
\NormalTok{new_date =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{cut}\NormalTok{(tweets_date, }\DataTypeTok{breaks =} \StringTok{"day"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{## Get the month and year}
\NormalTok{final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{new_date <-}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{new_date}
\NormalTok{final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{new_date =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.Date}\NormalTok{(final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{new_date, }\StringTok{"%Y-%m-%d"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{month_year =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{format}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{as.Date}\NormalTok{(final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{new_date), }\StringTok{"%b-%Y"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{get-date-country-and-app}{%
\subsubsection{Get date, country and
app}\label{get-date-country-and-app}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{data <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{month_year, final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{country, final_data}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{app_name)}
\KeywordTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(data)<-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"date"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"country"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"app"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{data}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}

\hypertarget{plot-the-tweets-collected-per-month-per-country}{%

country}\label{plot-the-tweets-collected-per-month-per-country}}

\CommentTok{#tiff("test.tiff", units="in", width=5, height=5, res=300)}
\KeywordTok{ggplot}\NormalTok{(data_country, }\KeywordTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{reorder}\NormalTok{(date, n), }\DataTypeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ n, }\DataTypeTok{fill=}\NormalTok{country)) }\OperatorTok{+}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{geom_col}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{position =} \StringTok{"dodge"}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{alpha =} \FloatTok{0.9}\NormalTok{) }\OperatorTok{+}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{theme_bw}\NormalTok{() }\OperatorTok{+}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{theme}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{axis.text.x=}\KeywordTok{element_text}\NormalTok{(}\DataTypeTok{angle =} \DecValTok{-90}\NormalTok{, }\DataTypeTok{hjust =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)) }\OperatorTok{+}
\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{xlab}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Period"}\NormalTok{) }\OperatorTok{+}

\subsection{Merge country and app and get the count w.r.t
date}\label{merge-country-and-app-and-get-the-count-w.r.t-date}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

\StringTok{  }\KeywordTok{add_count}\NormalTok{(date)}

\NormalTok{df <-}\StringTok{  }\NormalTok{df }\OperatorTok{%>%}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{distinct}\NormalTok{()}
